SELECT [a0].[Id], [d].[Name] AS [DeviceName], [z].[Name] AS [ZoneName], CASE [a0].[Type]
    WHEN 1 THEN N'HighConsumption'
    WHEN 2 THEN N'Anomaly'
    WHEN 3 THEN N'Wastage'
    WHEN 4 THEN N'DeviceOffline'
    ELSE CAST([a0].[Type] AS nvarchar(max))
END AS [AlertType], [a0].[Message], [a0].[Severity], CASE
    WHEN [a0].[Severity] = 1 THEN N'Info'
    WHEN [a0].[Severity] = 2 THEN N'Warning'
    ELSE N'Critical'
END AS [SeverityLabel], CASE
    WHEN [a0].[Severity] = 1 THEN N'🔵'
    WHEN [a0].[Severity] = 2 THEN N'🟡'
    ELSE N'🔴'
END AS [Icon], [a0].[CreatedAt], [a0].[IsRead]

SELECT [a0].[Id], [d].[Name] AS [DeviceName], [z].[Name] AS [ZoneName], CASE [a0].[Type]
    WHEN 1 THEN N'HighConsumption'
    WHEN 2 THEN N'Anomaly'
    WHEN 3 THEN N'Wastage'
    WHEN 4 THEN N'DeviceOffline'
    ELSE CAST([a0].[Type] AS nvarchar(max))
END AS [AlertType], [a0].[Message], [a0].[Severity], CASE
    WHEN [a0].[Severity] = 1 THEN N'Info'
    WHEN [a0].[Severity] = 2 THEN N'Warning'
    ELSE N'Critical'
END AS [SeverityLabel], CASE
    WHEN [a0].[Severity] = 1 THEN N'🔵'
    WHEN [a0].[Severity] = 2 THEN N'🟡'
    ELSE N'🔴'
END AS [Icon], [a0].[CreatedAt], [a0].[IsRead]
FROM (
    SELECT [a].[Id], [a].[CreatedAt], [a].[DeviceId], [a].[IsRead], [a].[Message], [a].[Severity], [a].[Type]
    FROM [Alerts] AS [a]
    WHERE [a].[CreatedAt] >= @__start_0 AND [a].[CreatedAt] <= @__end_1 AND [a].[IsRead] = @__isRead_Value_2
    ORDER BY [a].[CreatedAt] DESC
    OFFSET @__p_3 ROWS FETCH NEXT @__p_4 ROWS ONLY
) AS [a0]
INNER JOIN [Devices] AS [d] ON [a0].[DeviceId] = [d].[Id]
INNER JOIN [Zones] AS [z] ON [d].[ZoneId] = [z].[Id]
ORDER BY [a0].[CreatedAt] DESC
